 Reliance Industries on Thursday withdrew the notice of postponement of supply of natural gas to four fertilizer factories in Uttar Pradesh
 company ne kaha he ki vah bakaayaa ke mudde ko sulajhane ke liye uria companiyon ke saath milakar kaam karegi

 reliance ne in companiyon se rajya briki kar ke mad main vittiya guarantee badhaane ko kaha tha

 The war between RJD President Lalu Prasad Yadav and senior BJP leader Sushil Kumar Modi is going on with regard to the land gift issue
 lalu yadav ne susheel modi par manahani kaa mukaddama daayar karne kii dhamkee di to susheel modi ne jawaab main kah daalaa ki jiskaa maan sammaan hoga vahi manahani kaa mukaddama kar saktaa he
 In fact, the case is about getting land donated from BJP MP Rama Devi to Lalu's elder Tej Pratap Yadav
 1992 main lalu yadav ke mantrimandal main brajabihari prasad shaamil the
 Rama Devi is the wife of Brajbihari
 susheel modi ne aarope lagaaya tha ki jab tejpratap 4 saal ke the tab unhen 13 acre 12 dismil jameen rama devi ne daan main di thi
 On the allegation of Sushil Modi, Laloo Yadav said that he had canceled the registry of the land
 phir susheel modi aisa aarope kyon laga rahe hai
 Lalu asked Sushil Modi to apologize, terming the allegations as baseless
 cancil kyon karai registry?lalu ke is jawaab par susheel modi phir palatwaar kiya
 Sushil Modi asked why Lalu Yadav got the registry canceled after 15 months
 unhone lalu se sawaal kiya ki kya wo raghunatha jha, kanti singh, lalan choudhary, hridayanand choudhary or prabhunath subhash se gift ke rup main liye gaye makaan or jameen bhi waapas denge
 Sushil Modi claimed, "since Rama Devi's land belonged to the rural area, she returned it
" magar lalan choudhary or hridayanand kii jameen shahari ilaakon kii he, isliye rakh lee
 On the matter, Rama Devi had said that she had gifted land at the behest of her husband
 haalanki, rama devi ne jab jameen gift kii thi tab wo sakriy raajnneeti main nahin thim
 Please tell that there are eight ponds on this land
 jisamen machhali paalan kiya jaataa he
 Rama Devi keeps the entire account of the land
 jameen kii dekharekh karne vaale munna pandey bataate hai ki 20 saal se jameen kaa hisaab rama devi ke hi paas he
 Shivji Rai, the landowner, said, "he had heard that the land had been given to Lalu Yadav's son, but the land was withdrawn after differences with Brijbihari
 ''susheel kumaar modi lagaataar lalu ke parivaar par aarope laga rahe hai
 On the other hand, in many cases of benami property, the CBI and ED have also raided the premises of Lalu's family
 yahaan tak ki lalu kii beti misa bharti se poochtacha bhi kii ja chuki he
 The Congress, which has so far refrained from directly attacking the SP over the communal violence in Muzaffarnagar district of Uttar Pradesh, has demanded the resignation of the state Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav

 10
 bihar kaa janata dal united or orissa kaa biju janata dal jaise kshetreey dal jiesti ke prastaav par utsuk hai
 States like Bihar, Odisha are not large industrial producers
 unhen vishwaas he ki jiesti se unako laabh hoga
 1
 jiesti main kendriya bikri kar or centre va rajya ke levi kaa vilay kiya ja rahaa he
 It is an attempt to create a common market for one billion people from 29 states of the country
 2
 The Lok Sabha has approved the tax reform bill
 ab sarkaar ise rajyasabha main, jahaan ki vah alpamat main he, paarit karaane ke liye prayatnsheel he
 After this the proposal has to be approved in more than half of the 29 states, which is a long process
 3
 Finance Minister Arun Jaitley has set a deadline of 1 April 2016 to implement GST
 is sthiti main yah aavashyak ho jaataa he ki yah vidheyak guuruuvaar ko samaapt hone vaale monsoon satr main hi paarit ho jaae
 4) Regarding GST, the Finance Minister says that this will be the biggest tax reform in India
 unhone aashaa jataai he ki isse bhartiya arthvyavastha do pratishat kii vruddhi ke saath asia kii teesri sabase badi arthvyavastha ban jaaegi
 5) Government is of the opinion that GST will make the functioning of industries easier
 isamen pratispardhaa ke saath rajyon main nirmaan ko protsaahan milegaa
 It is visionary for more efficient delivery of goods and services to consumers and lowering prices
 6
 Experts, on the other hand, say that in the states concerned with losing revenue in many areas, the GST proposal includes several agreements
 udhaaharan ke liye sharaab par kar lagu nahin hota he or petroleum bhi rajya ke daayre se baahar rakhaa gaya he
 Currently, states can levy local taxes at their own level
 7
 States are allowed to levy an additional one percent interstate levy for two years
 8
 The government brought the GST bill in the Rajya Sabha on Tuesday, but the Congress flatly refused to discuss it
 congress ne kaha ki She will not discuss until the government finds External Affairs Minister Sushma Swaraj guilty of helping tainted cricket tycoon Lalit Modi
 tippaniyan 9
 sarkaar is vidheyak ko paarit karaane ke liye chote dalon kaa sahaara lene main juty he
 The government has sought support from Tamil Nadu Chief Minister j Jayalalithaa
 chennai main pichley saptaah pradhanmantri ne ek lunch baithak main annadramuk ke 11 rajyasabha saansadon se charchaa kii
 The AIADMK has been opposing the bill till now
 10
 Regional parties like Bihar's Janata Dal United and Odisha's Biju Janata Dal are keen on the GST proposal
 bihar, orissa jaise rajya bade audyogic utpaadak nahin hai
 They are confident that they will benefit from GST

 bhopal sthit mausam vibhaag centre ke mutabik is saal 18 sitambar tak 1688
 There was 9 mm of rain
 mausam vigyaanik jidi mishra ke mutabik bhopal mausam vibhaag centre ke paas saal 1980 se 2019 ke bich kaa jo aankada uplabdh he uske mutabik is saal bhopal main sabase zyada barish record kii gai he
 According to meteorologist GD Mishra, 1686 in the year 2006
